This table lists all C++ committee documents for 2016, 2017, 2018, and 2019. Each document is identified by its WG21 document number, title, author (or authors) and date. The month of the mailing in which the document was distributed is also given. For a revised document, the numbers of the previous revision are given. Technical papers are classified by working group. Finally, when a technical paper (other than an issue list) is revised or formally adopted, an indication is provided.
